<h2 id="examples" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#examples"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Examples</h2>
<h3 id="basic" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#basic"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Basic</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Display a user&#x27;s profile image with a fallback.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_4fhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_4fhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_4fhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="events" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#events"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Events</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">onStatusChange</code> to listen for loading state changes.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_4lhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_4lhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_4lhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="root-provider" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#root-provider"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Root Provider</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">An alternative way to control the avatar is to use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">RootProvider</code> component and the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">useAvatar</code> hook. This way you
can access the state and methods from outside the component.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_4rhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_4rhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_4rhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h2 id="guides" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#guides"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Guides</h2>
<h3 id="nextjs-image" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#nextjs-image"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Next.js Image</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Here&#x27;s an example of how to use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Image</code> component from <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">next/image</code>.</p>
<pre class="fs_0.875em lh_1.7142857 mt_1.7142857em mb_1.7142857em bdr_0.375rem p_4 color-scheme_dark [&amp;_code]:bg-c_transparent [&amp;_code]:bd-w_0 [&amp;_code]:bdr_0 [&amp;_code]:p_0 [&amp;_code]:fw_inherit [&amp;_code]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_inherit [&amp;_code]:ff_inherit [&amp;_code]:lh_inherit shiki github-dark-default" style="background-color:#0d1117;color:#e6edf3" tabindex="0"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2"><span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">import</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> { Avatar, useAvatarContext } </span><span style="color:#FF7B72">from</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF"> &#x27;@ark-ui/react/avatar&#x27;</span></span>

<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">const</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF"> AvatarNextImage</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> =</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> (</span><span style="color:#FFA657">props</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">:</span><span style="color:#FFA657"> ImageProps</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">) </span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=&gt;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">  const</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> avatar</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> =</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF"> useAvatarContext</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">()</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">  const</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> { </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">hidden</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">, </span><span style="color:#FF7B72">...</span><span style="color:#79C0FF">arkImageProps</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> } </span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> avatar.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">getImageProps</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">()</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">  const</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> nextImage</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> =</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF"> getImageProps</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(props)</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">  return</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> (</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">    &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">img</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">      {...</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">arkImageProps</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">}</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">      {...</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">nextImage.props</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">}</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF">      style</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">={</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">{</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">        ...</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">props.style,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#8B949E">        // use visibility instead</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">        visibility: hidden </span><span style="color:#FF7B72">?</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF"> &#x27;hidden&#x27;</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> :</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF"> &#x27;visible&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">      }</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">}</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">    /&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  )</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">}</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">const</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF"> Demo</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> =</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> () </span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=&gt;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">  return</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> (</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">    &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Avatar.Root</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">      &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Avatar.Fallback</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;JD&lt;/</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Avatar.Fallback</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">      &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">AvatarNextImage</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> src</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&quot;...&quot;</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> alt</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&quot;&quot;</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> width</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">={</span><span style="color:#79C0FF">80</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">}</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> height</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">={</span><span style="color:#79C0FF">80</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">}</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> /&gt;</span></span>

<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  )</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">}</span></span></code></pre>
<blockquote class="mt_1.6em mb_1.6em ps_1em fw_500 font-style_italic bd-s-w_0.25rem bd-c_var(--colors-prose-quote-border)">
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Refer to this <a target="_blank" rel="noopener" href="https://github.com/chakra-ui/ark/discussions/3147" class="link">Github Discussion</a> for more information.</p>
</blockquote>
<h2 id="api-reference" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#api-reference"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>API Reference</h2>

Anatomy\n\n\u003cAnatomy id=\"avatar\" /\u003e\n\n```tsx\n\u003cAvatar.Root\u003e\n  \u003cAvatar.Fallback /\u003e\n  \u003cAvatar.Image /\u003e\n\u003c/Avatar.Root\u003e\n```\n\n## Examples\n\n### Basic\n\nDisplay a user's profile image with a fallback.\n\n**Example: basic**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Avatar } from '@ark-ui/react/avatar'\nimport styles from 'styles/avatar.module.css'\n\nexport const Basic = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cAvatar.Root className={styles.Root}\u003e\n    \u003cAvatar.Fallback className={styles.Fallback}\u003ePA\u003c/Avatar.Fallback\u003e\n    \u003cAvatar.Image className={styles.Image} src=\"https://i.pravatar.cc/300?u=a\" alt=\"avatar\" /\u003e\n  \u003c/Avatar.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Avatar } from '@ark-ui/solid/avatar'\nimport styles from 'styles/avatar.module.css'\n\nexport const Basic = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cAvatar.Root class={styles.Root}\u003e\n    \u003cAvatar.Fallback class={styles.Fallback}\u003ePA\u003c/Avatar.Fallback\u003e\n    \u003cAvatar.Image class={styles.Image} src=\"https://i.pravatar.cc/300?u=a\" alt=\"avatar\" /\u003e\n  \u003c/Avatar.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Avatar } from '@ark-ui/vue/avatar'\nimport styles from 'styles/avatar.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cAvatar.Root :class=\"styles.Root\"\u003e\n    \u003cAvatar.Fallback :class=\"styles.Fallback\"\u003ePA\u003c/Avatar.Fallback\u003e\n    \u003cAvatar.Image :class=\"styles.Image\" src=\"https://i.pravatar.cc/300?u=a\" alt=\"avatar\" /\u003e\n  \u003c/Avatar.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Avatar } from '@ark-ui/svelte/avatar'\n  import styles from 'styles/avatar.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cAvatar.Root class={styles.Root}\u003e\n  \u003cAvatar.Fallback class={styles.Fallback}\u003ePA\u003c/Avatar.Fallback\u003e\n  \u003cAvatar.Image class={styles.Image} src=\"https://i.pravatar.cc/300?u=a\" alt=\"avatar\" /\u003e\n\u003c/Avatar.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Events\n\nUse `onStatusChange` to listen for loading state changes.\n\n**Example: events**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Avatar } from '@ark-ui/react/avatar'\nimport { useState } from 'react'\nimport styles from 'styles/avatar.module.css'\n\nexport const Events = () =\u003e {\n  const [status, setStatus] = useState('loading...')\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv className=\"vstack\"\u003e\n      \u003coutput\u003eStatus: {status}\u003c/output\u003e\n      \u003cAvatar.Root className={styles.Root} onStatusChange={(e) =\u003e setStatus(e.status)}\u003e\n        \u003cAvatar.Fallback className={styles.Fallback}\u003ePA\u003c/Avatar.Fallback\u003e\n        \u003cAvatar.Image className={styles.Image} src=\"https://i.pravatar.cc/3000?u=a\" alt=\"avatar\" /\u003e\n      \u003c/Avatar.Root\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Avatar } from '@ark-ui/solid/avatar'\nimport { createSignal } from 'solid-js'\nimport styles from 'styles/avatar.module.css'\n\nexport const Events = () =\u003e {\n  const [status, setStatus] = createSignal('loading...')\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv class=\"vstack\"\u003e\n      \u003coutput\u003eStatus: {status()}\u003c/output\u003e\n      \u003cAvatar.Root class={styles.Root} onStatusChange={(e) =\u003e setStatus(e.status)}\u003e\n        \u003cAvatar.Fallback class={styles.Fallback}\u003ePA\u003c/Avatar.Fallback\u003e\n        \u003cAvatar.Image class={styles.Image} src=\"https://i.pravatar.cc/3000?u=a\" alt=\"avatar\" /\u003e\n      \u003c/Avatar.Root\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Avatar } from '@ark-ui/vue/avatar'\nimport { ref } from 'vue'\nimport styles from 'styles/avatar.module.css'\n\nconst status = ref('loading...')\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cdiv class=\"vstack\"\u003e\n    \u003coutput\u003eStatus: {{ status }}\u003c/output\u003e\n    \u003cAvatar.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" @status-change=\"(e) =\u003e (status = e.status)\"\u003e\n      \u003cAvatar.Fallback :class=\"styles.Fallback\"\u003ePA\u003c/Avatar.Fallback\u003e\n      \u003cAvatar.Image :class=\"styles.Image\" src=\"https://i.pravatar.cc/3000?u=a\" alt=\"avatar\" /\u003e\n    \u003c/Avatar.Root\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Avatar } from '@ark-ui/svelte/avatar'\n  import styles from 'styles/avatar.module.css'\n\n  let status = $state('loading...')\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cdiv class=\"vstack\"\u003e\n  \u003coutput\u003eStatus: {status}\u003c/output\u003e\n  \u003cAvatar.Root class={styles.Root} onStatusChange={(e) =\u003e (status = e.status)}\u003e\n    \u003cAvatar.Fallback class={styles.Fallback}\u003ePA\u003c/Avatar.Fallback\u003e\n    \u003cAvatar.Image class={styles.Image} src=\"https://i.pravatar.cc/3000?u=a\" alt=\"avatar\" /\u003e\n  \u003c/Avatar.Root\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Root Provider\n\nAn alternative way to control the avatar is to use the `RootProvider` component and the `useAvatar` hook. This way you\ncan access the state and methods from outside the component.\n\n**Example: root-provider**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Avatar, useAvatar } from '@ark-ui/react/avatar'\nimport { useState } from 'react'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/avatar.module.css'\n\nexport const RootProvider = () =\u003e {\n  const [count, setCount] = useState(0)\n  const avatar = useAvatar()\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv className=\"vstack\"\u003e\n      \u003cbutton className={button.Root} onClick={() =\u003e setCount(count + 1)}\u003e\n        Change Avatar\n      \u003c/button\u003e\n\n      \u003cAvatar.RootProvider className={styles.Root} value={avatar}\u003e\n        \u003cAvatar.Fallback className={styles.Fallback}\u003ePA\u003c/Avatar.Fallback\u003e\n        \u003cAvatar.Image className={styles.Image} src={`https://i.pravatar.cc/300?u=${count}`} alt=\"avatar\" /\u003e\n      \u003c/Avatar.RootProvider\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Avatar, useAvatar } from '@ark-ui/solid/avatar'\nimport { createSignal } from 'solid-js'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/avatar.module.css'\n\nexport const RootProvider = () =\u003e {\n  const [count, setCount] = createSignal(0)\n  const avatar = useAvatar()\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv class=\"vstack\"\u003e\n      \u003cbutton class={button.Root} onClick={() =\u003e setCount(count() + 1)}\u003e\n        Change Avatar\n      \u003c/button\u003e\n\n      \u003cAvatar.RootProvider class={styles.Root} value={avatar}\u003e\n        \u003cAvatar.Fallback class={styles.Fallback}\u003ePA\u003c/Avatar.Fallback\u003e\n        \u003cAvatar.Image class={styles.Image} src={`https://i.pravatar.cc/300?u=${count()}`} alt=\"avatar\" /\u003e\n      \u003c/Avatar.RootProvider\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Avatar, useAvatar } from '@ark-ui/vue/avatar'\nimport { ref } from 'vue'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/avatar.module.css'\n\nconst count = ref(0)\nconst avatar = useAvatar()\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cdiv class=\"vstack\"\u003e\n    \u003cbutton :class=\"button.Root\" @click=\"count++\"\u003eChange Avatar\u003c/button\u003e\n\n    \u003cAvatar.RootProvider :class=\"styles.Root\" :value=\"avatar\"\u003e\n      \u003cAvatar.Fallback :class=\"styles.Fallback\"\u003ePA\u003c/Avatar.Fallback\u003e\n      \u003cAvatar.Image :class=\"styles.Image\" :src=\"`https://i.pravatar.cc/300?u=${count}`\" alt=\"avatar\" /\u003e\n    \u003c/Avatar.RootProvider\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Avatar, useAvatar } from '@ark-ui/svelte/avatar'\n  import button from 'styles/button.module.css'\n  import styles from 'styles/avatar.module.css'\n\n  const id = $props.id()\n  const avatar = useAvatar({ id })\n\n  let counter = $state(0)\n  const src = $derived(`https://i.pravatar.cc/300?u=${counter}`)\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cdiv class=\"vstack\"\u003e\n  \u003cbutton class={button.Root} onclick={() =\u003e counter++}\u003eChange Avatar\u003c/button\u003e\n\n  \u003cAvatar.RootProvider class={styles.Root} value={avatar}\u003e\n    \u003cAvatar.Fallback class={styles.Fallback}\u003ePA\u003c/Avatar.Fallback\u003e\n    \u003cAvatar.Image class={styles.Image} {src} alt=\"avatar\" /\u003e\n  \u003c/Avatar.RootProvider\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\n```\n\n## Guides\n\n### Next.js Image\n\nHere's an example of how to use the `Image` component from `next/image`.\n\n```tsx\nimport { Avatar, useAvatarContext } from '@ark-ui/react/avatar'\nimport { getImageProps, type ImageProps } from 'next/image'\n\nconst AvatarNextImage = (props: ImageProps) =\u003e {\n  const avatar = useAvatarContext()\n\n  const { hidden, ...arkImageProps } = avatar.getImageProps()\n  const nextImage = getImageProps(props)\n\n  return (\n    \u003cimg\n      {...arkImageProps}\n      {...nextImage.props}\n      style={{\n        ...props.style,\n        // use visibility instead\n        visibility: hidden ? 'hidden' : 'visible',\n      }}\n    /\u003e\n  )\n}\n\nconst Demo = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cAvatar.Root\u003e\n      \u003cAvatar.Fallback\u003eJD\u003c/Avatar.Fallback\u003e\n      \u003cAvatarNextImage src=\"...\" alt=\"\" width={80} height={80} /\u003e\n    \u003c/Avatar.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n```\n\n\u003e Refer to this [Github Discussion](https://github.com/chakra-ui/ark/discussions/3147) for more information.\n\n## API Reference\n\n### Props\n\n**Component API Reference**\n\n#### React\n\n**Root Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `boolean` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n| `ids` | `Partial\u003c{ root: string; image: string; fallback: string }\u003e` | No | The ids of the elements in the avatar. Useful for composition. |\n| `onStatusChange` | `(details: StatusChangeDetails) =\u003e void` | No | Functional called when the image loading status changes. |\n\n\n**Fallback Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `boolean` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n\n\n**Fallback Data Attributes:**\n\n| Attribute | Value |\n|-----------|-------|\n| `[data-scope]` | avatar |\n| `[data-part]` | fallback |\n| `[data-state]` | \"hidden\" | \"visible\" |\n\n\n**Image Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `boolean` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n\n\n**Image Data Attributes:**\n\n| Attribute | Value |\n|-----------|-------|\n| `[data-scope]` | avatar |\n| `[data-part]` | image |\n| `[data-state]` | \"visible\" | \"hidden\" |\n\n\n**RootProvider Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `value` | `UseAvatarReturn` | Yes |  |\n| `asChild` | `boolean` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n\n\n#### Solid\n\n**Root Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `(props: ParentProps\u003c'div'\u003e) =\u003e Element` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n| `ids` | `Partial\u003c{ root: string; image: string; fallback: string }\u003e` | No | The ids of the elements in the avatar. Useful for composition. |\n| `onStatusChange` | `(details: StatusChangeDetails) =\u003e void` | No | Functional called when the image loading status changes. |\n\n\n**Fallback Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `(props: ParentProps\u003c'span'\u003e) =\u003e Element` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n\n\n**Fallback Data Attributes:**\n\n| Attribute | Value |\n|-----------|-------|\n| `[data-scope]` | avatar |\n| `[data-part]` | fallback |\n| `[data-state]` | \"hidden\" | \"visible\" |\n\n\n**Image Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `(props: ParentProps\u003c'img'\u003e) =\u003e Element` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n\n\n**Image Data Attributes:**\n\n| Attribute | Value |\n|-----------|-------|\n| `[data-scope]` | avatar |\n| `[data-part]` | image |\n| `[data-state]` | \"visible\" | \"hidden\" |\n\n\n**RootProvider Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `value` | `UseAvatarReturn` | Yes |  |\n| `asChild` | `(props: ParentProps\u003c'div'\u003e) =\u003e Element` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n\n\n#### Vue\n\n**Root Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `boolean` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n| `id` | `string` | No | The unique identifier of the machine. |\n| `ids` | `Partial\u003c{ root: string; image: string; fallback: string }\u003e` | No | The ids of the elements in the avatar. Useful for composition. |\n\n\n**Fallback Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `boolean` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n\n\n**Fallback Data Attributes:**\n\n| Attribute | Value |\n|-----------|-------|\n| `[data-scope]` | avatar |\n| `[data-part]` | fallback |\n| `[data-state]` | \"hidden\" | \"visible\" |\n\n\n**Image Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `boolean` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n\n\n**Image Data Attributes:**\n\n| Attribute | Value |\n|-----------|-------|\n| `[data-scope]` | avatar |\n| `[data-part]` | image |\n| `[data-state]` | \"visible\" | \"hidden\" |\n\n\n**RootProvider Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `value` | `AvatarApi\u003cPropTypes\u003e` | Yes |  |\n| `asChild` | `boolean` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n\n\n#### Svelte\n\n**Root Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `Snippet\u003c[PropsFn\u003c'div'\u003e]\u003e` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n| `id` | `string` | No | The unique identifier of the machine. |\n| `ids` | `Partial\u003c{ root: string; image: string; fallback: string }\u003e` | No | The ids of the elements in the avatar. Useful for composition. |\n| `onStatusChange` | `(details: StatusChangeDetails) =\u003e void` | No | Functional called when the image loading status changes. |\n| `ref` | `Element` | No |
